***перемешать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a> (13733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешать.html>меша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peremešátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешивать.html>переме́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stir, to agitate</li>
<li>to intermix, to intermingle, to mix <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">together, with</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to blend <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to shuffle, to mix up, to confuse, to jumble up, to muddle up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peremešátʹ</b> kárty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>shuffle/mix</b> the cards</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peremešátʹ</b> vse bumági na stolé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>mix/jumble up</b> all the papers on the table</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>у́гли</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>угли́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печка.html>пе́чке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peremešátʹ</b> úgli/uglí v péčke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>poke</b> the fire in a stove</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перемешаться.html>перемеша́ться</a> (21226)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peremešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешаться.html>перемеша́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peremešátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешиваться.html>переме́шиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become mixed up, to become confused, to become jumbled</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mix together, to mingle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of people or dissimilar objects</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peremešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***перемешивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перемешивать.html>переме́шивать</a> (29024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peremešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешивать.html>переме́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereméšivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешать.html>перемеша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stir, to agitate</li>
<li>to intermix, to intermingle, to mix <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">together, with</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to blend <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to shuffle, to mix up, to confuse, to jumble up, to muddle up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешивать.html>переме́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereméšivatʹ</b> kárty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>shuffle/mix</b> the cards</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешивать.html>переме́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereméšivatʹ</b> vse bumági na stolé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>mix/jumble up</b> all the papers on the table</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешивать.html>переме́шивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>у́гли</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>угли́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печка.html>пе́чке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereméšivatʹ</b> úgli/uglí v péčke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>poke</b> the fire in a stove</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешиваться.html>переме́шиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereméšivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешаться.html>перемеша́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become mixed up, to become confused, to become jumbled</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mix together, to mingle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of people or dissimilar objects</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перемешивать.html>переме́шивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereméšivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мина́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-minátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перенести.html>перенёсший</a> (2795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенести.html>перенёсший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenjósšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенести.html>перенести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perenestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенести.html>перенести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переносить.html>переноси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transfer, to carry, to transport</li>
<li><i>(word)</i> to carry over to the next line</li>
<li>to postpone, to put off</li>
<li>to extend</li>
<li>to bear, to endure, to stand, to survive, to withstand</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перенестись.html>перенести́сь</a> (20401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенести.html>перенести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perenestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенестись.html>перенести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переноситься.html>переноси́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move, to travel, to go <i>(very quickly)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to step
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перенестись.html>перенести́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысленно.html>мы́сленно</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́слях</a>) куда́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perenestísʹ</b> mýslenno (v mýsljax) kudá-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go somewhere in one's imagination</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенести.html>перенести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perenestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***перенимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перенимать.html>перенима́ть</a> (24646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенимать.html>перенима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенять.html>переня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to adopt, to imitate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перенимать.html>перенима́ть</a></b> че́й-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:опыт.html>о́пыт</a> (чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:метода.html>методы</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perenimátʹ</b> čéj-libo ópyt (čʹí-libo metody)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to adopt smb's practices / methods</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***перенос.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́с</a> (16645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenós</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>carrying over, transfer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perenós ognjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shift of fire</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poligraphy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informatics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> word division, hyphenation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правило.html>правила</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́са</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́в</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pravila <b>perenósa</b> slov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">word hyphenation rules</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>hyphen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расстановка.html>расстано́вка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́сов</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rasstanóvka <b>perenósov</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">hyphenation</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:необязательный.html>необяза́тельный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перенос.html>перено́с</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neobjazátelʹnyj <b>perenós</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">discretionary/optional hyphen</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>slippage, transfer, carry-forward</li></ol>

***переносить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переносить.html>переноси́ть</a> (4621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переносить.html>переноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перенести.html>перенести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transfer, to carry, to transport <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переносить.html>перено́сит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершенно.html>соверше́нно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On v mýsli <b>perenósit</b> sebjá v soveršénno drugój mir</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>transfers</b> himself mentally to a completely different world</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переносить.html>переноси́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:легкое.html>лёгкое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тело.html>те́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порог.html>поро́г</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>perenosíla</b> ljóxkoje télo čerez poróg</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She <b>carried</b> the lightweight body through the sill</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to carry over (a word) to the next line</li>
<li>to postpone, to put off</li>
<li>to extend <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to bear, to endure, to stand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переносить.html>переноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весьма.html>весьма́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стойкий.html>сто́йко</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perenosítʹ</b> vesʹmá stójko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">To endure very persistently</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переносить.html>переноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перена́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry (all or many things) from one place to another</li>
<li>to wear (all or many items of clothing)</li>
<li>to carry (a child) too long in a pregnancy</li></ol>

***переночевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переночевать.html>переночева́ть</a> (10248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночевать.html>ночева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nočevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переночевать.html>переночева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perenočevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to spend the night, to stay over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переночевать.html>переночева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гостиница.html>гости́нице</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perenočevátʹ</b> v gostínice</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stay over in a hotel</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The verb occurs transitively in the expression <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переночевать.html>переночева́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чь</a></span>.
</p>
